 The Aam Aadmi Party's Delhi government, concerned with air quality in the national capital Delhi, has directed the city's schools to install air purifiers to protect students from health-related diseases caused by air pollution
 shiksha nideshak neskulonse yah bhi kaha he ki ve andhadhundh pataakhe jalaane ke kaaran logon ke swasthya par padane vaale bure asar ke bare main chaatro ke bich jaagrukta failaaen
 Let us tell you that the order sent to schools on Friday said, Delhi's air quality needs to be improved
 hawa kii kharaab gunvattta ke kaaran maanav swasthya ko pahunchane vaale baari nuksaan ko dekhte hue skulon ko jarurat ke mutabik air filter lagane ke liye kadam uthaane chahie
 Significantly, the order also asked the schools to take appropriate steps to educate the students about the need to improve air quality
 isamen kaha gaya, padhai ke saath anya gatividhiyon ke jariye yuva peedi ke sahyog ko badhaava diya janaa chahie
 Schools have been asked to submit a report on compliance with this directive within 15 days

 If you are thinking of getting a tax exemption by buying a second house, just know the new rules of the budget 2017-18 of Finance Minister Arun Jaitley
 ab duusare ghar par tex main pehle jaisi chhot nahin milegi
 According to the new rules of the central government, you will be able to get a tax exemption of up to 2 lakh rupees on a home loan taken on a second home
 yani sarkaar un logon ko dheel nahin dena chaahati he jo ek se zyada property kharidkar home lone uthaa lete hai or uske jariye tex main chhot pate hai
 In the new rule, for the first time home buyers are given priority in tax exemption
 isamen un logon ko chhot nahin di gai he jo apane ghar main rahete hai or duusari property kharidkar usase kiraaya kama rahe hai
 Earlier the landlord could claim full exemption on the interest of the rented property, whereas the people living in their own house were entitled to claim up to Rs 2 lakh only
 haalanki bajet 2017-18 ke niyamon ke anusaar makaan kiraye par die jane par bhi 2 lakh rupee tak kii hi chhot kaa daawa kiya ja sakegaa
 That is, the person who built a house by taking a loan, can now claim the benefit of rebate up to Rs 2 lakh (whether he rents the house or stays in it)
 tippaniyan For example, the annual interest on EMI for another property in a particular year is Rs 5 lakh
 maan len koi makaan maalik 1
 An income of Rs 5 lakh makes a profit from that property throughout the year
 aise kharidaar, pehle ke niyam ke mutabik, kul 3
 You could have adjusted the income up to 5 lakhs, but now from the next financial year they will be able to take a discount of only 2 lakhs
 shesh 1
 5 lakhs can be carried forward for 8 years
 ashok maheshwari and associats elelpi main kar or niamak nideshak sandip sahagal ne bataaya ki ab tak log kiraaya kamaane ke lihaaj se hi duusari property kharidte the
 In this, they were also able to get tax exemption on home loan taken on another property, as well as earning rent from it
 isse unhen donon taraf se phayda hota tha, vahiin sarkaar ko do taraf se nuksaan uthaanaa pad rahaa tha
 To prevent this, the government has made a provision of a maximum tax exemption of Rs 2 lakh per annum on the home taken on other properties
 nae niyam main pehali baar ghar kharidne waalon ko tex chhot main praathamikta di ja rahi he
 It does not give exemption to those who live in their house and are earning rent by buying other property
 pehle makaan maalik kiraye par di gai property ke byaaj par puri chhot kaa daawa kar saktaa tha, jabaki apane makaan main khud rahane vaale 2 lakh rupee tak hi clem karne kaa hakdaar hote the
 However, according to the rules of the budget 2017-18, a rebate of up to Rs 2 lakh can be claimed even if the house is given on rent
 yani, jisane lone lekar makaan banaaya, vah ab har haal main (chaahe vah makaan ko kiraye par de de yaa usamen khud rahe) 2 lakh rupye tak kii chhot ke laabh kaa daawa kar sakegaa

 5 lakh tak kii aay ko samyojit kar sakate the, lekin ab agle vitt varsh se ve keval 2 lakh rupee kii chhot hi uthaa sakenge
 1 remaining 5 lakh ko 8 saal tak kairi forward kiya ja sakegaa

 ) The country's biggest identity scheme, the most ambitious project to cover the entire country in 12 digits

 The work of issuing unique identity card, ie Aadhar card, is going on in full swing in the country
 ab tak kareeb 12 karod logon ko yuaidi number jari bhi kiya ja chuke hai
 But before this, the most wanted and super advanced plan of UPA government could be raised, serious questions have started to arise
 is khulaase se aapke bhi hosh ud jaayenge ki kaise rajdhani dilli main emele or empi voton ke chakkar main desh kii suraksha ke saath samjhauta kar rahe hai
 Aajtak came to know that the country's largest identity card is being distributed without any identification, then Aaj Tak started investigating with the intelligence camera and a dangerous picture came out
 hamane janaa ki kaise koi videshi aantki bina kisi pareshaani ke bhartiya hone kii pahchaan aasaani se hasil kar saktaa he
 In fact, the Unique Identification Authority of India gave the local registrar the right to give exemption in the documents required to get the Aadhaar card made, which is being taken advantage of by local leaders in the circle of vote bank
 ye log yuaidi card banavaane kii jugat lage hai
 If there is no identity card, then we are in line for the certificate being distributed at Netaji's house
 netaji ke chamache bhi dhadadhad sin karne or thappa maarane main lage hai

 ab iske liye desh kii suraksha se samjhauta karne pade to bhala kise parvaah he

 ye hai 1
 Photo ID, 2
 janm tithi pramaan patr, 3
 residence certificate
 aise main asthaayee pate par rahane vaale logon kii pareshaani ko dekhte hue yuaidi athurity ne awaas pramaan patr ke liye sthaneey vidhayak or saansad ke dwaara jari kiye gayi pramaan patr ko manyata de di
 This rigging started just here
 janpratinidhiyon ne bina kisi jaan-pahchaan or veriphication ke latter had par awaas pramaan patr jari karnaa shuru kar diya

 jinako paane ke liye subah hote hi logon kii lambii qatari lag jaati he

 hamaara kaam ricomend karnaa he

 - film main kai saare moment bhi hai jo aakhir tak yaad rah jate hai
